FNV OMV AMBIENT OCCLUSION STATE AND CAPTURE CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. Which engine render states are established for a native image-space pass?
2. Can alpha test, stencil test, or scissor test remain active at 0x00876136?
3. Has current-frame first-person depth finished rendering before 0x00876136?
4. Is resolving first-person depth after Main::RenderFirstPerson necessarily too late for OMV scene-pre AO?
5. Which camera and rendered-texture objects are live at the image-space callsite?

Render-state mapping from the available engine headers:
  BSRS_ALPHA_TEST=4, BSRS_STENCIL_ENABLE=9, BSRS_SCISSOR_TEST=13
  BSRS_COLOR_WRITE=16, BSRS_FILL_MODE=18, BSRS_CULL_MODE=19

Static limitation:
This proves vanilla code shape only. Runtime GetRenderState telemetry is still required to show the exact inherited state on a blinking frame.
